\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    \usepackage[breakable]{tcolorbox}
    \usepackage{parskip} % Stop auto-indenting (to mimic markdown behaviour)
    

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % Keep aspect ratio if custom image width or height is specified
    \setkeys{Gin}{keepaspectratio}
    % Maintain compatibility with old templates. Remove in nbconvert 6.0
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionFormat{nocaption}{}
    \captionsetup{format=nocaption,aboveskip=0pt,belowskip=0pt}

    \usepackage{float}
    \floatplacement{figure}{H} % forces figures to be placed at the correct location
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro

    \usepackage{iftex}
    \ifPDFTeX
        \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
        \IfFileExists{alphabeta.sty}{
              \usepackage{alphabeta}
          }{
              \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs}
              \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc}
          }
    \else
        \usepackage{fontspec}
        \usepackage{unicode-math}
    \fi

    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics
                         % to support a larger range
    \makeatletter % fix for old versions of grffile with XeLaTeX
    \@ifpackagelater{grffile}{2019/11/01}
    {
      % Do nothing on new versions
    }
    {
      \def\Gread@@xetex#1{%
        \IfFileExists{"\Gin@base".bb}%
        {\Gread@eps{\Gin@base.bb}}%
        {\Gread@@xetex@aux#1}%
      }
    }
    \makeatother
    \usepackage[Export]{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size
    \adjustboxset{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}

    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    % The default LaTeX title has an obnoxious amount of whitespace. By default,
    % titling removes some of it. It also provides customization options.
    \usepackage{titling}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage{array}     % table support for pandoc >= 2.11.3
    \usepackage{calc}      % table minipage width calculation for pandoc >= 2.11.1
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines
    \usepackage{soul}      % strikethrough (\st) support for pandoc >= 3.0.0
    \usepackage{mathrsfs}

    \definecolor{urlcolor}{rgb}{0,.145,.698}

    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}

    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}

    % For linebreaks inside Verbatim environment from package fancyvrb.
    \makeatletter
        \newbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox
        \newbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox
        \newcommand*\Wrappedvisiblespace {\textcolor{red}{\textvisiblespace}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol {\textcolor{red}{\llap{\tiny$\m@th\hookrightarrow$}}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationindent {3ex }
        \newcommand*\Wrappedafterbreak {\kern\Wrappedcontinuationindent\copy\Wrappedcontinuationbox}
        % Take advantage of the already applied Pygments mark-up to insert
        % potential linebreaks for TeX processing.
        %        {, <, #, %, $, ' and ": go to next line.
        %        _, }, ^, &, >, - and ~: stay at end of broken line.
        % Use of \textquotesingle for straight quote.
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatspecials {%
            \def\PYGZus{\discretionary{\char`\_}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\_}}%
            \def\PYGZob{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\{}{\char`\{}}%
            \def\PYGZcb{\discretionary{\char`\}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\}}}%
            \def\PYGZca{\discretionary{\char`\^}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\^}}%
            \def\PYGZam{\discretionary{\char`\&}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\&}}%
            \def\PYGZlt{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\<}{\char`\<}}%
            \def\PYGZgt{\discretionary{\char`\>}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\>}}%
            \def\PYGZsh{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\#}{\char`\#}}%
            \def\PYGZpc{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\%}{\char`\%}}%
            \def\PYGZdl{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\$}{\char`\$}}%
            \def\PYGZhy{\discretionary{\char`\-}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\-}}%
            \def\PYGZsq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\textquotesingle}{\textquotesingle}}%
            \def\PYGZdq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\"}{\char`\"}}%
            \def\PYGZti{\discretionary{\char`\~}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\~}}%
        }
        % Some characters . , ; ? ! / are not pygmentized.
        % This macro makes them "active" and they will insert potential linebreaks
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatpunct {%
            \lccode`\~`\.\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\.}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\.}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\,\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\,}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\,}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\;\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\;}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\;}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\:\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\:}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\:}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\?\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\?}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\?}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\!\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\!}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\!}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\/\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\/}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\/}}}%
            \catcode`\.\active
            \catcode`\,\active
            \catcode`\;\active
            \catcode`\:\active
            \catcode`\?\active
            \catcode`\!\active
            \catcode`\/\active
            \lccode`\~`\~
        }
    \makeatother

    \let\OriginalVerbatim=\Verbatim
    \makeatletter
    \renewcommand{\Verbatim}[1][1]{%
        %\parskip\z@skip
        \sbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox {\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol}%
        \sbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox {\FV@SetupFont\Wrappedvisiblespace}%
        \def\FancyVerbFormatLine ##1{\hsize\linewidth
            \vtop{\raggedright\hyphenpenalty\z@\exhyphenpenalty\z@
                \doublehyphendemerits\z@\finalhyphendemerits\z@
                \strut ##1\strut}%
        }%
        % If the linebreak is at a space, the latter will be displayed as visible
        % space at end of first line, and a continuation symbol starts next line.
        % Stretch/shrink are however usually zero for typewriter font.
        \def\FV@Space {%
            \nobreak\hskip\z@ plus\fontdimen3\font minus\fontdimen4\font
            \discretionary{\copy\Wrappedvisiblespacebox}{\Wrappedafterbreak}
            {\kern\fontdimen2\font}%
        }%

        % Allow breaks at special characters using \PYG... macros.
        \Wrappedbreaksatspecials
        % Breaks at punctuation characters . , ; ? ! and / need catcode=\active
        \OriginalVerbatim[#1,codes*=\Wrappedbreaksatpunct]%
    }
    \makeatother

    % Exact colors from NB
    \definecolor{incolor}{HTML}{303F9F}
    \definecolor{outcolor}{HTML}{D84315}
    \definecolor{cellborder}{HTML}{CFCFCF}
    \definecolor{cellbackground}{HTML}{F7F7F7}

    % prompt
    \makeatletter
    \newcommand{\boxspacing}{\kern\kvtcb@left@rule\kern\kvtcb@boxsep}
    \makeatother
    \newcommand{\prompt}[4]{
        {\ttfamily\llap{{\color{#2}[#3]:\hspace{3pt}#4}}\vspace{-\baselineskip}}
    }
    

    
    % Prevent overflowing lines due to hard-to-break entities
    \sloppy
    % Setup hyperref package
    \hypersetup{
      breaklinks=true,  % so long urls are correctly broken across lines
      colorlinks=true,
      urlcolor=urlcolor,
      linkcolor=linkcolor,
      citecolor=citecolor,
      }
    % Slightly bigger margins than the latex defaults
    
    \geometry{verbose,tmargin=1in,bmargin=1in,lmargin=1in,rmargin=1in}
    
    

\begin{document}
    
    \maketitle
    
    

    
    \subsection*{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Homework
4}}{Homework 4}}\label{homework-4}

\textbf{Instructions} * This homework focuses on understanding and
applying CoCoOp for CLIP prompt tuning. It consists of \textbf{four
questions} designed to assess both theoretical understanding and
practical application.

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Please organize your answers and results for the questions below and
  submit this jupyter notebook as \textbf{a .pdf file}.
\item
  \textbf{Deadline: 11/26 (Sat) 23:59}
\end{itemize}

    \subsubsection*{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Preparation}}{Preparation}}\label{preparation}

\begin{itemize}

    \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM\PYZus{}VNET}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{LR\PYZus{}SCHEDULER} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{single\PYZus{}step}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}1 or 0 means the stepsize is equal to max\PYZus{}epoch}
    \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM\PYZus{}VNET}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{STEPSIZE} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM\PYZus{}VNET}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{GAMMA} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.1}
    \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM\PYZus{}VNET}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{MAX\PYZus{}EPOCH} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Set WARMUP\PYZus{}EPOCH larger than 0 to activate warmup training}
    \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM\PYZus{}VNET}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{WARMUP\PYZus{}EPOCH} \PY{o}{=} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Either linear or constant}
    \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM\PYZus{}VNET}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{WARMUP\PYZus{}TYPE} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{linear}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Constant learning rate when type=constant}
    \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM\PYZus{}VNET}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{WARMUP\PYZus{}CONS\PYZus{}LR} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{1e\PYZhy{}5}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Minimum learning rate when type=linear}
    \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM\PYZus{}VNET}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{WARMUP\PYZus{}MIN\PYZus{}LR} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{1e\PYZhy{}5}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Recount epoch for the next scheduler (last\PYZus{}epoch=\PYZhy{}1)}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Otherwise last\PYZus{}epoch=warmup\PYZus{}epoch}
    \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM\PYZus{}VNET}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{WARMUP\PYZus{}RECOUNT} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{True}

    \PY{n}{extend\PYZus{}cfg}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 1. From the dataset config file}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{args}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dataset\PYZus{}config\PYZus{}file}\PY{p}{:}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 2. From the method config file}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{args}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{config\PYZus{}file}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{merge\PYZus{}from\PYZus{}file}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{args}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{config\PYZus{}file}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. From input arguments}
    \PY{n}{reset\PYZus{}cfg}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{freeze}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{cfg}

\PY{n}{\PYZus{}tokenizer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{\PYZus{}Tokenizer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{load\PYZus{}clip\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}cpu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Load CLIP}
    \PY{n}{backbone\PYZus{}name} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{MODEL}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{BACKBONE}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{NAME}
    \PY{n}{url} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{clip}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}MODELS}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{backbone\PYZus{}name}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}path} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{clip}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}download}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{url}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{try}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} loading JIT archive}
        \PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{jit}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{map\PYZus{}location}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{cpu}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{eval}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}dict} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{None}

    \PY{k}{except} \PY{n+ne}{RuntimeError}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}dict} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{map\PYZus{}location}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{cpu}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{TRAINER}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{NAME} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}
      \PY{n}{design\PYZus{}trainer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{CoOp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
      \PY{n}{design\PYZus{}trainer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{TRAINER}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{NAME}
    \PY{n}{design\PYZus{}details} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{trainer}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{design\PYZus{}trainer}\PY{p}{,}
                      \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{vision\PYZus{}depth}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,}
                      \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{language\PYZus{}depth}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{vision\PYZus{}ctx}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,}
                      \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{language\PYZus{}ctx}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
    \PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{clip}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{build\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state\PYZus{}dict} \PY{o+ow}{or} \PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{state\PYZus{}dict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{design\PYZus{}details}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{model}

\PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{dassl}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{config} \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n}{get\PYZus{}cfg\PYZus{}default}

\PY{k}{class} \PY{n+nc}{TextEncoder}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Module}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{clip\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 초기화 하는 함수}
        \PY{n+nb}{super}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n+nf+fm}{\PYZus{}\PYZus{}init\PYZus{}\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{transformer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{clip\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{transformer}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{positional\PYZus{}embedding} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{clip\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{positional\PYZus{}embedding}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ln\PYZus{}final} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{clip\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ln\PYZus{}final}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{text\PYZus{}projection} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{clip\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{text\PYZus{}projection}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dtype} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{clip\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dtype}

    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{forward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{prompts}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{tokenized\PYZus{}prompts}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 모델 호출}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prompts} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{positional\PYZus{}embedding}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dtype}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{x}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{permute}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} NLD \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} LND}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{transformer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{x}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{permute}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} LND \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} NLD}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ln\PYZus{}final}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dtype}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} x.shape = [batch\PYZus{}size, n\PYZus{}ctx, transformer.width]}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} take features from the eot embedding (eot\PYZus{}token is the highest number in each sequence)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{arange}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{tokenized\PYZus{}prompts}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{argmax}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dim}\PY{o}{=}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{@} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{text\PYZus{}projection}

        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{x}


\PY{n+nd}{@TRAINER\PYZus{}REGISTRY}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{register}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{force}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{class} \PY{n+nc}{CoCoOp}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{TrainerX}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{check\PYZus{}cfg}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{assert} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{TRAINER}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{COCOOP}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{PREC} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{fp16}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{fp32}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{amp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{build\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{cfg} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cfg}
        \PY{n}{classnames} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dataset}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{classnames}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Loading CLIP (backbone: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{MODEL}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{BACKBONE}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{NAME}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{clip\PYZus{}model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{load\PYZus{}clip\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}cpu}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{TRAINER}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{COCOOP}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{PREC} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{fp32}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o+ow}{or} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{TRAINER}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{COCOOP}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{PREC} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{amp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} CLIP\PYZsq{}s default precision is fp16}
            \PY{n}{clip\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{float}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Building custom CLIP}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{CoCoOpCustomCLIP}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{classnames}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{clip\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Turning off gradients in both the image and the text encoder}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{name\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}update} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{prompt\PYZus{}learner}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}

        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{param} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{named\PYZus{}parameters}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{name\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}update} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n}{param}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{requires\PYZus{}grad\PYZus{}}\PY{p}{(}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Double check}
        \PY{n}{enabled} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{set}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{param} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{named\PYZus{}parameters}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{param}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{requires\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{n}{enabled}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Parameters to be updated: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{enabled}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{MODEL}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{INIT\PYZus{}WEIGHTS}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{load\PYZus{}pretrained\PYZus{}weights}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{prompt\PYZus{}learner}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{MODEL}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{INIT\PYZus{}WEIGHTS}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} NOTE: only give prompt\PYZus{}learner to the optimizer}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{optim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{build\PYZus{}optimizer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{prompt\PYZus{}learner}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sched} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{build\PYZus{}lr\PYZus{}scheduler}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{optim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OPTIM}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{register\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{prompt\PYZus{}learner}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{prompt\PYZus{}learner}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{optim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sched}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{scaler} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{GradScaler}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{TRAINER}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{COCOOP}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{PREC} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{amp}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{else} \PY{k+kc}{None}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Note that multi\PYZhy{}gpu training could be slow because CLIP\PYZsq{}s size is}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} big, which slows down the copy operation in DataParallel}
        \PY{n}{device\PYZus{}count} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cuda}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{device\PYZus{}count}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{device\PYZus{}count} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Multiple GPUs detected (n\PYZus{}gpus=}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{device\PYZus{}count}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{), use all of them!}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{DataParallel}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{before\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{directory} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{OUTPUT\PYZus{}DIR}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{RESUME}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{directory} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{RESUME}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{start\PYZus{}epoch} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{resume\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}if\PYZus{}exist}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{directory}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Remember the starting time (for computing the elapsed time)}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{time\PYZus{}start} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{time}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{time}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}


    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{forward\PYZus{}backward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{batch}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{image}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{label} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{parse\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{batch}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model}
        \PY{n}{optim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{optim}
        \PY{n}{scaler} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{scaler}

        \PY{n}{prec} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{TRAINER}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{COCOOP}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{PREC}
        \PY{n}{loss} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{image}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{label}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Input image 모델 통과}
        \PY{n}{optim}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{zero\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{backward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Backward (역전파)}
        \PY{n}{optim}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{step}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 모델 parameter update}

        \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}summary} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{loss}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{item}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}

        \PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}idx} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{num\PYZus{}batches}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{update\PYZus{}lr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{loss\PYZus{}summary}

    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{parse\PYZus{}batch\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{batch}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n+nb}{input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{batch}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{img}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{label} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{batch}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{label}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n+nb}{input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{input}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{label} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{label}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{device}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n+nb}{input}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{label}

    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{load\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{directory}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{epoch}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{directory}\PY{p}{:}

            \PY{k}{return}

        \PY{n}{names} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}model\PYZus{}names}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} By default, the best model is loaded}

        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{name} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{names}\PY{p}{:}

            \PY{k}{if} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n}{osp}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{exists}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{k}{raise} \PY{n+ne}{FileNotFoundError}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Model not found at }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

            \PY{n}{checkpoint} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{load\PYZus{}checkpoint}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}dict} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{checkpoint}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{state\PYZus{}dict}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{n}{epoch} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{checkpoint}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{epoch}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}

            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Ignore fixed token vectors}
            \PY{k}{if} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{token\PYZus{}prefix}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}dict}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{k}{del} \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}dict}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{token\PYZus{}prefix}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}

            \PY{k}{if} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{token\PYZus{}suffix}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}dict}\PY{p}{:}
                \PY{k}{del} \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}dict}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{token\PYZus{}suffix}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}

            \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Loading weights to }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{from }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ (epoch = }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{format}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{model\PYZus{}path}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{epoch}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} set strict=False}
            \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}models}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load\PYZus{}state\PYZus{}dict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state\PYZus{}dict}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{strict}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{after\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
      \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Finish training}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

      \PY{n}{do\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{TEST}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{NO\PYZus{}TEST}
      \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{do\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{:}
          \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{TEST}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{FINAL\PYZus{}MODEL} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{best\PYZus{}val}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Deploy the model with the best val performance}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{load\PYZus{}model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{output\PYZus{}dir}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Deploy the last\PYZhy{}epoch model}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{acc} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{test}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

      \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Show elapsed time}
      \PY{n}{elapsed} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{time}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{time}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{time\PYZus{}start}\PY{p}{)}
      \PY{n}{elapsed} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{str}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{datetime}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{timedelta}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{seconds}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{elapsed}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
      \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Elapsed: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{elapsed}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

      \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Close writer}
      \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{close\PYZus{}writer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
      \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{acc}

    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{train}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
\PY{+w}{        }\PY{l+s+sd}{\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}Generic training loops.\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{before\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{for} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{epoch} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{start\PYZus{}epoch}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{max\PYZus{}epoch}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{before\PYZus{}epoch}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{run\PYZus{}epoch}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
            \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{after\PYZus{}epoch}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{acc} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{after\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{acc}

\PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{main}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{cfg} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{setup\PYZus{}cfg}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{args}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{SEED} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}}\PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{set\PYZus{}random\PYZus{}seed}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{SEED}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cuda}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{is\PYZus{}available}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{USE\PYZus{}CUDA}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{backends}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cudnn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{benchmark} \PY{o}{=} \PY{k+kc}{True}

    \PY{n}{trainer} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{build\PYZus{}trainer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cfg}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{args}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{eval\PYZus{}only}\PY{p}{:}

    \subsubsection*{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Q1. Understanding and
implementing
CoCoOp}}{Q1. Understanding and implementing CoCoOp}}\label{q1.-understanding-and-implementing-cocoop}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  We have learned how to define CoOp in Lab Session 4.
\item
  The main difference between CoOp and CoCoOp is \textbf{meta network}
  to extract image tokens that is added to the text prompt.
\item
  Based on the CoOp code given in Lab Session 4, fill-in-the-blank
  exercise to test your understanding of critical parts of the CoCoOp.
\end{itemize}

            \PY{n}{ctx\PYZus{}vectors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{embedding}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}ctx}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{n}{prompt\PYZus{}prefix} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{ctx\PYZus{}init}
        \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} random initialization}
            \PY{n}{ctx\PYZus{}vectors} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{empty}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}ctx}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ctx\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dtype}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{dtype}\PY{p}{)}

            \PY{n}{prompt\PYZus{}prefix} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{join}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{X}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}ctx}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Initial context: }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{prompt\PYZus{}prefix}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Number of context words (tokens): }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}ctx}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ctx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Parameter}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{ctx\PYZus{}vectors}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Wrap the initialized prompts above as parameters to make them trainable.}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{} Tokenize \PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}}
        \PY{n}{classnames} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{name}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZus{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{name} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{classnames}\PY{p}{]}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 예) \PYZdq{}Forest\PYZdq{}}
        \PY{n}{name\PYZus{}lens} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{\PYZus{}tokenizer}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{encode}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{name}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{name} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{classnames}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{prompts} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{prompt\PYZus{}prefix} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ }\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{name} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{.}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{name} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{classnames}\PY{p}{]} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 예) \PYZdq{}A photo of Forest.\PYZdq{}}

        \PY{n}{tokenized\PYZus{}prompts} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cat}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{clip}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{tokenize}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{p} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{prompts}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 예) [49406, 320, 1125, 539...]}



        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{} Q1. Fill in the blank \PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{} Define Meta Net \PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{meta\PYZus{}net} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Sequential}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{OrderedDict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{[}
            \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}(\PYZdq{}linear1\PYZdq{}, \PYZdq{}fill in here\PYZdq{}(vis\PYZus{}dim, vis\PYZus{}dim // 16)),}
            \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{linear1}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Linear}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{vis\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{vis\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{/}\PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{16}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{relu}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ReLU}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{inplace}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{linear2}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{nn}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{Linear}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{vis\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{/}\PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{16}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ctx\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{}}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}\PYZsh{} Hint: meta network is composed to linear layer, relu activation, and linear layer.}



        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{cfg}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{TRAINER}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{COCOOP}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{PREC} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{fp16}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{meta\PYZus{}net}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{half}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{with} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{no\PYZus{}grad}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{embedding} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{clip\PYZus{}model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{token\PYZus{}embedding}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{tokenized\PYZus{}prompts}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{type}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dtype}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} These token vectors will be saved when in save\PYZus{}model(),}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} but they should be ignored in load\PYZus{}model() as we want to use}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} those computed using the current class names}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{register\PYZus{}buffer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{token\PYZus{}prefix}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{embedding}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} SOS}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{register\PYZus{}buffer}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{token\PYZus{}suffix}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{embedding}\PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}ctx}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{,} \PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} CLS, EOS}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}cls} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}cls}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}ctx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}ctx}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{tokenized\PYZus{}prompts} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tokenized\PYZus{}prompts}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} torch.Tensor}
        \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{name\PYZus{}lens} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{name\PYZus{}lens}

    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{construct\PYZus{}prompts}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ctx}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{prefix}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{suffix}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{label}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} dim0 is either batch\PYZus{}size (during training) or n\PYZus{}cls (during testing)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ctx: context tokens, with shape of (dim0, n\PYZus{}ctx, ctx\PYZus{}dim)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} prefix: the sos token, with shape of (n\PYZus{}cls, 1, ctx\PYZus{}dim)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} suffix: remaining tokens, with shape of (n\PYZus{}cls, *, ctx\PYZus{}dim)}

        \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{label} \PY{o+ow}{is} \PY{o+ow}{not} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{:}
            \PY{n}{prefix} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prefix}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{label}\PY{p}{]}
            \PY{n}{suffix} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{suffix}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{label}\PY{p}{]}

        \PY{n}{prompts} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{torch}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{cat}\PY{p}{(}
            \PY{p}{[}
                \PY{n}{prefix}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} (dim0, 1, dim)}
                \PY{n}{ctx}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} (dim0, n\PYZus{}ctx, dim)}
                \PY{n}{suffix}\PY{p}{,}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} (dim0, *, dim)}
            \PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{n}{dim}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{p}{)}

        \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{prompts}

    \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{forward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{im\PYZus{}features}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{prefix} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{token\PYZus{}prefix}
        \PY{n}{suffix} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{token\PYZus{}suffix}
        \PY{n}{ctx} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ctx}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} (n\PYZus{}ctx, ctx\PYZus{}dim)}

    \subsubsection*{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{Q3. Analyzing the results of
CoCoOp}}{Q3. Analyzing the results of CoCoOp}}\label{q3.-analyzing-the-results-of-cocoop}

Compare the results of CoCoOp with those of CoOp that we trained in Lab
Session 4. Discuss possible reasons for the performance differences
observed between CoCoOp and CoOp.

    CoCoOp outperforms CoOp on base classes with an accuracy of 90.8\%, but
performs worse on novel classes with 43.3\% accuracy. This is because
CoCoOp's adaptive prompt-learning is highly optimized for base classes
but struggles to generalize to novel classes. In contrast, CoOp's fixed
prompts ensure stable performance across both classes but lack
flexibility. While CoCoOp excels in base class performance, improvements
like regularization or hybrid approaches are needed to enhance its
generalization for novel classes.
